<div id="review_114912946" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/114912946" />
    <a title="Shelley" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3081722-shelley"><img alt="Shelley" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1420295300p2/3081722.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/114912946?book_show_action=true">Aug 02, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shelley" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shelley" href="/user/show/3081722-shelley">Shelley</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3081722-shelley?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3081722-shelley?shelf=2010-release">2010-release</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer114912946" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7337567858955464896">Faythe represents a rare and important minority in her species; a tabby, or female cat shifter. There are certain expectations of her within the Pride; she's expected to marry in order to reproduce children and be subjugated to the male dominated environment for which she exists. Her spouse will also represent the next Alpha, taking the place of her father.<br/><br/>Following events in Stray, she becomes the first ever female enforcer; an exclusive band of fighters that serve the Alpha and protect their P</span>
  <span id="freeText7337567858955464896" style="display:none">Faythe represents a rare and important minority in her species; a tabby, or female cat shifter. There are certain expectations of her within the Pride; she's expected to marry in order to reproduce children and be subjugated to the male dominated environment for which she exists. Her spouse will also represent the next Alpha, taking the place of her father.<br /><br />Following events in Stray, she becomes the first ever female enforcer; an exclusive band of fighters that serve the Alpha and protect their Pride. Her father is grooming her to inherit his place as Alpha, a concept that won't be easily acheived or accepted by the larger cat community. In the mean time Faythe is juggling her romantic relationship with Marc, a fellow enforcer, who is forever pressing her for a commitment as well as keen interest from Jace.<br /><br />The plot heats up when Faythe recieves cryptic phone calls from her college boyfriend, Andrew, an ordinary human, who is now threatening her. He's also been turned into a shifter by Faythe after a minor sexual encounter before she left college. She's also investigating the murder of several cats on pride territory, and a possible link between these and enemies introduced in Stray. <br /><br />On top of that, women start going missing and tom cats end up mysteriously dead. Faythe discovers that it is far more sinister than realized. She then begins to understand that it may all be her fault since Andrew is part of the pack that is doing the killing.<br /><br />I like Ethan, one of Faythe's brothers, even though clearly he is a party animal and has had numerous relationships with women. I also like Michael and Owen, her other brothers. Michael is the family lawyer and also has a human wife. I also found Faythe's mother to be intriguing and someone you can look up to. I still don't like Marc. I don't like the way he treats Faythe, especially after learning she might have scratched and turned Andrew. <br /><br />Faythe still has some growing up to do, and she is truly annoying at times. Good thing this is only the second book in the series. I liked the first book, but this one is definitely alot better.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7337567858955464896" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_27024563" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/27024563" />
    <a title="Tez" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1090898-tez"><img alt="Tez" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1208410826p2/1090898.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/27024563?book_show_action=true">Jul 12, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tez" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tez" href="/user/show/1090898-tez">Tez</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer27024563&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer27024563" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14817908322198756939">Two killers are on the loose in Rachel Vincent's second Shifters novel, <u>Rogue</u>.<br/><br/>The Southcentral Pride has been tipped off about murdered toms, and this tests Faythe Sanders in her newly promoted role as an enforcer. Add that to investigating the recent spate of murdered strippers, and she has a lot on her plate. Then there are the spooky calls from her human ex...<br/><br/>It all doesn't bode well for Faythe's relationship with Marc Ramos, a needy, clingy, violent individual who won't let Faythe defend her</span>
  <span id="freeText14817908322198756939" style="display:none">Two killers are on the loose in Rachel Vincent's second Shifters novel, <u>Rogue</u>.<br /><br />The Southcentral Pride has been tipped off about murdered toms, and this tests Faythe Sanders in her newly promoted role as an enforcer. Add that to investigating the recent spate of murdered strippers, and she has a lot on her plate. Then there are the spooky calls from her human ex...<br /><br />It all doesn't bode well for Faythe's relationship with Marc Ramos, a needy, clingy, violent individual who won't let Faythe defend herself. That may seem romantic to some, but seems way too controlling and whingey to me. Give a lass some freaking space, man! And a promise ring doesn't count as freaking space...<br /><br />Excuse the relationship, and this book is quite a cracker. Rachel Vincent has well and truly mastered the art of the end-of-chapter cliffhanger...and likewise for the end of the novel. To discuss plot points would be major spoilers, so I'll just say "wow" and leave it at that. But I rather enjoyed the extra light shed on Karen Sanders, Faythe's mother and someone she doesn't seem to respect. There's also a new character I'm hoping (and expecting) will be featured more in the next installment. Suddenly I don't feel so bad about taking so long to actually get around to reading this, because now it's only a month until <u>Pride</u>'s February 1st release date - huzzah!<br /><br />Faythe continues to make mistakes and grow up, but one question remains: will those broken doors ever be fixed?</span>
  <a data-text-id="14817908322198756939" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/155887709?book_show_action=true">Mar 21, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danny" href="/user/show/3254909-danny">Danny</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3254909-danny?shelf=audiobooks">audiobooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3254909-danny?shelf=march-2011">march-2011</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer155887709" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16880549856028469649">One of those series where the second book even gets better.. I liked the intensity of this one. The conflicts of Marc and Faythe were sometimes absolutely heartbreaking! <br/><br/>Faythe is finally home and is working for her father as an enforcer together with Marc as a Team. But when they start to discover dead Toms and Faythe is getting angry calls from her human Ex (in both ways Ex..) things are getting heavy really fast. <br/><br/>Apart from the suspense that runs always along, the relationship between the cha</span>
  <span id="freeText16880549856028469649" style="display:none">One of those series where the second book even gets better.. I liked the intensity of this one. The conflicts of Marc and Faythe were sometimes absolutely heartbreaking! <br /><br />Faythe is finally home and is working for her father as an enforcer together with Marc as a Team. But when they start to discover dead Toms and Faythe is getting angry calls from her human Ex (in both ways Ex..) things are getting heavy really fast. <br /><br />Apart from the suspense that runs always along, the relationship between the characters is what catches me the most. Honestly, I love Faythe but I was also angry with her so so so often!! I wanted to scream at her and slap her to get back to her senses. Specially, together with Marc. <br />Oh my Marc! He is such a wonderful strong but also heartbreakingly soft character who loves Faythe so deeply it hurts. She doesn't deserve him - absolutely not! <br /><br />There is one scene that made me cry: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ when Marc asked Faythe to wear his promise ring and she again refused! I was cheering for him when he said "Thanking you for giving me my balls back" <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />The ending made me just start the next one right away! <br /><br />Some word about the audio: I love the narrator she has an easy voice and I love her male interpretations. She did a pretty good job and I will continue listen to them! </span>
  <a data-text-id="16880549856028469649" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nNwZxLXiqfgP4FogNXldyyh7PNTfy2DyI4gh6e3dFkg7v0wlUTcxFaWaNUfxfKB0ckpLhE3eanbAPv18O1f/sQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('o9lwZf3a4XRQA2Y8usg+/7laCpOY8J7ggDjidv5m50sEuiWEGQ95mfp5CVt+zcNA42t9wwrllGRjjj7jKOwOsg==')})
  }
//]]>
